class="cl-8ad22182">Fighting continued intermittently for 15 months.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad2540e"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">No</span><span class="cl-8ad22182"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22182">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ad25423"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">3.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25422"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">The Allies had secured control over the regions around the two northern ports but did not attempt to march on Saint Petersburg; and the Red Army lacked the power to push them into the sea.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25422"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">No</span><span class="cl-8ad22182"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22182">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ad25418"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">3.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad2540e"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">The military stalemate and the harsh Russian winter took their toll on the morale of Allied troops.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad2540e"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">No</span><span class="cl-8ad22182"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22182">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ad25423"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">3.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25422"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">Their evacuation was scheduled for the spring of 1919; but fighting continued through the summer.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25422"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">No</span><span class="cl-8ad22182"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22182">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8ad25437"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">3.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25436"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22182">The withdrawal of Allied forces was completed on 27 September 1919, with Russia the victor by default, as in Russian Civil War I.There was no global organization at the time of the termination of this crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8ad25436"><p class="cl-8ad22db2"><span class="cl-8ad22196">Russian</span><span class="cl-8ad22196"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22196">Soviet</span><span class="cl-8ad22196"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22196">Federative</span><span class="cl-8ad22196"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22196">Socialist</span><span class="cl-8ad22196"> </span><span class="cl-8ad22196">Republic</span><span class="cl-8ad22182">.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>

class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Austria-Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Romania;Czechoslovakia</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">initiated</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">border</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">violation</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">toward</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8aefba62"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">France, concerned with strengthening Russia's western neighbors, tacitly encouraged the partition of Hungary.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">No</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8aefba80"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">The Mihly Krolyi-led government in Budapest was not recognized by France, the U.K., or the U.S.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">No</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8aefba62"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">International pressure on Hungary reached its peak on 20 March 1919 in the form of an ultimatum from the Supreme Council's delegate in Budapest, Lieutenant-Colonel Fernand Vix, to Krolyi: in accordance with a 26 February Paris Peace Conference decision the Hungarian government was instructed to accept the implementation of a neutral zone between Hungary and Romania.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef778c">France</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">initiated</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">ultimatum</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">toward</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"><br></span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">That</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">the</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">following</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">will</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">happen</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">France</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">initiated</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">invasion/occupation</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">toward</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">If</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">the</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">following</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">does</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">not</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">happen</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">NA</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8aefba80"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.10</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">The ultimatum triggered a crisis for Hungary because of the following: it threatened the loss of extensive Hungarian territory, even more than indicated in the November 1918 Armistice; there was intense time pressure -- 30 hours -- for acceptance; and because Vix, exceeding his orders, threatened military reprisals if the ultimatum were rejected.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">experienced</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">a</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">start</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">of</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">crisis</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">about</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">sentence</span><span class="cl-8aef778c"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">9</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8aefba62"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.11</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">Krolyi responded to a perceived threat to Hungary's existence by rejecting the ultimatum and by resigning in favor of the pro-Soviet Socialist Bla Kun.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba58"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">initiated</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">reject</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">Hungary</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">initiated</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef778c">institutions</span><span class="cl-8aef7782">6.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">The ultimatum and the response increased the risk of war in Central Europe.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef7782">No</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8aef7782">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr attacked from the north.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8aefba76"><p class="cl-8aef83b2"><span class="cl-8aef778c">Czechoslovakia</span><span class="cl-8aef7782"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">formal</span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">agreement;unspecified</span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">cooperation</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">toward</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">France</span><span class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d898">As with Italy in the Smyrna crisis, France began to occupy its assigned area in November 1919, taking control of the three main cities -- Maras, Aintab, and Urfa.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230ad4"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">France</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">initiated</span><span </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">area</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8b230ae0"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d898">11.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230adf"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">Turkey</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">experienced</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">crisis</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">about</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">sentence</span><span notably at the Erzurum and Sivas congresses in July-August and September.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230ad4"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">Turkey</span><span of Anatolia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230adf"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d898">No</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b230ad4"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d898">The Sublime Porte, the government of the Ottoman Empire in Constantinople, was reduced to an empty shell.)</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230ad4"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d898">No</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr France.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b230adf"><p class="cl-8b22e3ba"><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">France</span><span class="cl-8b22d898"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d898">experienced</span><span </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">act</span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">in</span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2"> </span><span class="cl-8b22d8a2">this</span><span style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8b2bb329"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">12.16</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb328"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">This blunt criticism was elaborated two days later by a carrot-stick dmarche from one ally to another: British Foreign Secretary Curzon told French Ambassador Cambon that, if France admitted it had erred in acting unilaterally and if it promised to refrain from such actions in the future, the U.K. would consider the matter "cleared up." Premier Millerand, who considered Anglo-French solidarity more important than the temporary presence of German troops in the Ruhr, gave the necessary assurances on 11 April, with a reciprocal German announcement the same day that all German forces in the Ruhr not required to put down the rebellion would be withdrawn immediately.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb328"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">France</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">initiated</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">accept</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">toward</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"><br></span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">United</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">Kingdom</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">.</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">NA</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8b2bb31f"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">12.17</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb31e"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">Then on 24 April Germany informed France that its troops in the Ruhr were being withdrawn thereby terminating France's crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb31e"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">No</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8b2bb329"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">12.18</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb328"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">On the 26th, at the San Remo Conference, Millerand agreed to withdraw French forces as soon as German troops were evacuated.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb328"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">France</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span ending Germany's crisis and the international crisis as a whole.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb31e"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">Germany</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">experienced</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">a</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">end</span><span France and Germany perceived the outcome as a victory.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b2bb328"><p class="cl-8b2b87ae"><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">France;Germany</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">experienced</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82">a</span><span class="cl-8b2b7c82"> </span><span class="cl-8b2b7c8c">victory</span><span was awarded a border 200 kilometers east of the old Curzon Line.</span></p></td><td class="cl-8b34bf90"><p class="cl-8b34933a"><span class="cl-8b348796">Russian</span><span class="cl-8b348796"> </span><span class="cl-8b4dd016">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-8b4e104e"><p class="cl-8b4ddc32"><span class="cl-8b4dd016">15.12</span></p></td><td
